The app settings support a variety of uses, including in tablets as digital photo frames.\r\n\r\nA Pro version upgrade is available as an in-app purchase - this includes a thumbnail view, transition effects and video support. The Pro upgrade is required to play videos, and supports many common video formats, including the extensions mp4, m4v,mkv, mts, m2ts, avi, mov, webm, wmv, mpg, mpeg and mpe (but support also depends on the encoding used within these files).\r\n\r\nThis app was formerly known as Basic Photo Viewer, and is still simple to use but is no longer quite so basic!\r\n\r\n[HEIC and WebP images may require the Windows 10 October 2018 Update. RAW format support depends on the camera model. Support for raf, rw2 and mrw files is limited to a few camera models.
